
#BUILDINGS
	#Production Methods:
	# Base
	# Industrialized (1800-60)
	# Mechanized (1880-90)
	# Modernized (1900-30)
	# Automatized (1950-90), not included

	# I    Basic (Pre-Industrial)
	# II   Advanced (1800s-1820s)
	# III  Industrialized (1830s-50s)
	# IV   Mechanized (1860s-80s)
	# V    Electrified (1890s-1910s)
	# VI   Motorized (1920s-40s)
	# VII  Modernized (1950s-60s)
	# VIII Roboticized (1970s-80s)
	# IX   Computerized (1990s-2000s)
	# X    Digitalized (2010s-2020s)
	# XI   Automatized (2030s-2040s)
	# XII  Futurized (2050s)

#Industries

	#arable_land
	#deposits@token:industry_
	#size@token:industry_

	increase_industry_by_x = {
		# x_temp, industry_token
		# State
		# This effect increases the size of the industry by x and updates all relevant information. 
		# 
		# To Strat: This should NOT be used internally but only as part of effects from focuses/events/others which take 
		#           effect in-between monthly pulses and not be used in the monthly pulse itself

	}
	construct_x_industries = {
		# x_temp, industry_token
		# State
		# This effect adds x to the under industries construction and adds them to the list if necessary
		# Negative numbers are allowed (and decreasing them to 0 or beyond will delete said industry if its size 0)

		construct_x_industries_no_update = yes
		industries_update_construction = yes
		ROOT = {
			refresh_industry_list = yes
			refresh_construction_list = yes
		}
	}
	construct_x_industries_no_update = {
		# x_temp, industry_token
		# State

		#Add industry to array if it doesn't exist yet
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_in_array = { industries = industry_token } }
			}
			add_to_array = { industries = industry_token }
		}

		add_to_variable = { under_construction@var:industry_token = x_temp }
		add_to_variable = { construction_amount@var:industry_token = global.industry_base_construction_amount@var:industry_token }

		#Construction
			set_temp_variable = { const_r = global.industry_base_construction_resource@var:industry_token }

			set_variable = { construction_speed@var:industry_token = global.industry_base_construction_speed@var:industry_token }
			multiply_variable = { construction_speed@var:industry_token = under_construction@var:industry_token }

			set_variable = { construction_expenses@var:industry_token = construction_speed@var:industry_token }
			multiply_variable = { construction_expenses@var:industry_token = price@var:const_r }
		#
	}
	create_industry = {
		#Input: industry_token (token)

		add_to_array = { industries = industry_token }

		#Buttons
		set_variable = { priority@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { subsidy@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { expansion@var:industry_token = 0 }

		#Employees
		set_variable = { employment_target@var:industry_token = 1 }
		set_variable = { employment_percentage@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { jobs@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { laborers_jobs@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { workers_jobs@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { professionals_jobs@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { elites_jobs@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { employed@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { laborers_employed@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { workers_employed@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { professionals_employed@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { elites_employed@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { laborers_payroll@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { workers_payroll@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { professionals_payroll@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { elites_payroll@var:industry_token = 0 }

		#Money
		set_variable = { money@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { money_limit@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { revenue@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { revenue_goods@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { revenue_subsidies@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { expenses@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { expenses_maintenance@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { expenses_input@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { expenses_payroll@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { expenses_bonuses@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { profit@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { profitability@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { productivity@var:industry_token = 0 }

		#Production
		set_variable = { size@var:industry_token = 1 }
		set_variable = { production@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { max_production@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { production_percentage@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { production_method@var:industry_token = 0 }

		#Inputs
		set_variable = { input_1_amount@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { input_1_expenses@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { input_2_amount@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { input_2_expenses@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { input_3_amount@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { input_3_expenses@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { input_4_amount@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { input_4_expenses@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { input_5_amount@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { input_5_expenses@var:industry_token = 0 }

		#Maintenance
		set_variable = { maintenance_1_amount@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { maintenance_1_expenses@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { maintenance_2_amount@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { maintenance_2_expenses@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { maintenance_3_amount@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { maintenance_3_expenses@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { maintenance_4_amount@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { maintenance_4_expenses@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { maintenance_5_amount@var:industry_token = 0 }
		set_variable = { maintenance_5_expenses@var:industry_token = 0 }

	}


	change_industry_avg_wage = {
		#wage_change_temp, industry_token

		set_temp_variable = { total_wage_multiplier = 0 }

		set_temp_variable = { wage_multiplier = laborers_employed@var:industry_token }
		multiply_temp_variable = { wage_multiplier = 2 }
		add_to_temp_variable = { total_wage_multiplier = wage_multiplier }

		set_temp_variable = { wage_multiplier = workers_employed@var:industry_token }
		multiply_temp_variable = { wage_multiplier = 5 }
		add_to_temp_variable = { total_wage_multiplier = wage_multiplier }

		set_temp_variable = { wage_multiplier = professionals_employed@var:industry_token }
		multiply_temp_variable = { wage_multiplier = 10 }
		add_to_temp_variable = { total_wage_multiplier = wage_multiplier }

		set_temp_variable = { wage_multiplier = elites_employed@var:industry_token }
		multiply_temp_variable = { wage_multiplier = 25 }
		add_to_temp_variable = { total_wage_multiplier = wage_multiplier }

		set_temp_variable = { ciw_wage = wage_change_temp }
		multiply_temp_variable = { ciw_wage = employed@var:industry_token }
		divide_temp_variable = { ciw_wage = total_wage_multiplier }
		
		add_to_variable = { base_wage@var:industry_token = ciw_wage }
	}
	change_industry_base_wage = {
		#wage_change_temp, industry_token

		add_to_variable = { base_wage@var:industry_token = wage_change_temp }
	}

	change_industry_employment_by_x_percent = {
		#x_percent_temp, industry_token
		add_to_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = employment_percentage@var:industry_token }

		set_industry_employment_to_x_percent = yes
	}
	set_industry_employment_to_x_percent = {
		#x_percent_temp, industry_token
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { x_percent_temp > 1 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { x_percent_temp < 0 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = 0 }
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = 100 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = 0.5 }
		round_temp_variable = x_percent_temp
		divide_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = 100 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = employment_percentage@var:industry_token }

		#Prospective Hiring
		set_temp_variable = { laborers_to_hire = laborers_jobs@var:industry_token }
		multiply_temp_variable = { laborers_to_hire = x_percent_temp }
		set_temp_variable = { workers_to_hire = workers_jobs@var:industry_token }
		multiply_temp_variable = { workers_to_hire = x_percent_temp }
		set_temp_variable = { professionals_to_hire = professionals_jobs@var:industry_token }
		multiply_temp_variable = { professionals_to_hire = x_percent_temp }
		set_temp_variable = { elites_to_hire = elites_jobs@var:industry_token }
		multiply_temp_variable = { elites_to_hire = x_percent_temp }

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { laborers_to_hire > laborers_unemployed_amount }
			}
			# Recorrecting Hiring %
			set_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = laborers_unemployed_amount }
			divide_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = laborers_jobs@var:industry_token }
			multiply_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = 100 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = 0.5 }
			round_temp_variable = x_percent_temp
			divide_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = 100 }

			# Redoing Prospective Hiring
			set_temp_variable = { workers_to_hire = workers_jobs@var:industry_token }
			multiply_temp_variable = { workers_to_hire = x_percent_temp }
			set_temp_variable = { professionals_to_hire = professionals_jobs@var:industry_token }
			multiply_temp_variable = { professionals_to_hire = x_percent_temp }
			set_temp_variable = { elites_to_hire = elites_jobs@var:industry_token }
			multiply_temp_variable = { elites_to_hire = x_percent_temp }

			set_temp_variable = { prod_break = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { workers_to_hire > workers_unemployed_amount }
			}
			# Recorrecting Hiring %
			set_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = workers_unemployed_amount }
			divide_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = workers_jobs@var:industry_token }
			multiply_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = 100 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = 0.5 }
			round_temp_variable = x_percent_temp
			divide_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = 100 }

			# Redoing Prospective Hiring
			set_temp_variable = { professionals_to_hire = professionals_jobs@var:industry_token }
			multiply_temp_variable = { professionals_to_hire = x_percent_temp }
			set_temp_variable = { elites_to_hire = elites_jobs@var:industry_token }
			multiply_temp_variable = { elites_to_hire = x_percent_temp }

			set_temp_variable = { prod_break = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { professionals_to_hire > professionals_unemployed_amount }
			}
			# Recorrecting Hiring %
			set_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = professionals_unemployed_amount }
			divide_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = professionals_jobs@var:industry_token }
			multiply_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = 100 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = 0.5 }
			round_temp_variable = x_percent_temp
			divide_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = 100 }

			# Redoing Prospective Hiring
			set_temp_variable = { elites_to_hire = elites_jobs@var:industry_token }
			multiply_temp_variable = { elites_to_hire = x_percent_temp }

			set_temp_variable = { prod_break = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { elites_to_hire > elites_unemployed_amount }
			}
			# Recorrecting Hiring %
			set_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = elites_unemployed_amount }
			divide_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = elites_jobs@var:industry_token }
			multiply_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = 100 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = 0.5 }
			round_temp_variable = x_percent_temp
			divide_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = 100 }

			set_temp_variable = { prod_break = 1 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { x_percent_temp = 0 } }
			}
			add_to_variable = { employment_percentage@var:industry_token = x_percent_temp }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { employment_percentage@var:industry_token < 0 }
				}
				set_variable = { employment_percentage@var:industry_token = 0 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { employment_percentage@var:industry_token > 1 }
				}
				set_variable = { employment_percentage@var:industry_token = 1 }
			}

			set_temp_variable = { laborers_before = laborers_employed@var:industry_token }
			set_temp_variable = { workers_before = workers_employed@var:industry_token }
			set_temp_variable = { professionals_before = professionals_employed@var:industry_token }
			set_temp_variable = { elites_before = elites_employed@var:industry_token }

			set_variable = { laborers_employed@var:industry_token = laborers_jobs@var:industry_token }
			multiply_variable = { laborers_employed@var:industry_token = employment_percentage@var:industry_token }
			set_variable = { workers_employed@var:industry_token = workers_jobs@var:industry_token }
			multiply_variable = { workers_employed@var:industry_token = employment_percentage@var:industry_token }
			set_variable = { professionals_employed@var:industry_token = professionals_jobs@var:industry_token }
			multiply_variable = { professionals_employed@var:industry_token = employment_percentage@var:industry_token }
			set_variable = { elites_employed@var:industry_token = elites_jobs@var:industry_token }
			multiply_variable = { elites_employed@var:industry_token = employment_percentage@var:industry_token }

			add_to_variable = { laborers_employed_amount = laborers_employed@var:industry_token }
			subtract_from_variable = { laborers_employed_amount = laborers_before }
			subtract_from_variable = { laborers_unemployed_amount = laborers_employed@var:industry_token }
			add_to_variable = { laborers_unemployed_amount = laborers_before }
			add_to_variable = { workers_employed_amount = workers_employed@var:industry_token }
			subtract_from_variable = { workers_employed_amount = workers_before }
			subtract_from_variable = { workers_unemployed_amount = workers_employed@var:industry_token }
			add_to_variable = { workers_unemployed_amount = workers_before }
			add_to_variable = { professionals_employed_amount = professionals_employed@var:industry_token }
			subtract_from_variable = { professionals_employed_amount = professionals_before }
			subtract_from_variable = { professionals_unemployed_amount = professionals_employed@var:industry_token }
			add_to_variable = { professionals_unemployed_amount = professionals_before }
			add_to_variable = { elites_employed_amount = elites_employed@var:industry_token }
			subtract_from_variable = { elites_employed_amount = elites_before }
			subtract_from_variable = { elites_unemployed_amount = elites_employed@var:industry_token }
			add_to_variable = { elites_unemployed_amount = elites_before }
		}
	}

	industries_update = {
		#State Scope
		#Updates each industry

		set_variable = { industries_jobs_amount = 0 }
		set_variable = { industries_employees_amount = 0 }
		set_variable = { industrial_power = 0 }

		for_each_loop = {
			array = industries
			value = iu_token
			index = ind
			break = ind_break

			industry_update = yes

			add_to_variable = { industries_jobs_amount = jobs@var:iu_token }
			add_to_variable = { industries_employees_amount = employed@var:iu_token }

			set_temp_variable = { ip_temp = global.base_price@var:iu_resource }
			multiply_temp_variable = { ip_temp = production@var:iu_token }
			add_to_variable = { industrial_power = ip_temp }
		}
	}
	industries_update_workforce = {
		#State Scope
		#Updates each industry's finances

		for_each_loop = {
			array = industries
			value = iu_token
			index = ind
			break = ind_break

			industry_update_workforce = yes
		}
	}
	industries_update_production = {
		#State Scope
		#Updates each industry's finances

		for_each_loop = {
			array = industries
			value = iu_token
			index = ind
			break = ind_break

			industry_update_production = yes
		}
	}
	industries_update_finances = {
		#State Scope
		#Updates each industry's finances

		for_each_loop = {
			array = industries
			value = iu_token
			index = ind
			break = ind_break

			industry_update_finances = yes
		}
	}

	industry_update = {
		#iu_token

		industry_update_workforce = yes
		industry_update_production = yes
		industry_update_finances = yes
	}
	industry_update_workforce = {
		#iu_token

		#Jobs Amount
			if = { #Base
				limit = {
					check_variable = { production_method@var:iu_token = 0 }
				}
				set_variable = { laborers_jobs@var:iu_token = global.industry_base_laborers_employment@var:iu_token }
				set_variable = { workers_jobs@var:iu_token = global.industry_base_workers_employment@var:iu_token }
				set_variable = { professionals_jobs@var:iu_token = global.industry_base_professionals_employment@var:iu_token }
				set_variable = { elites_jobs@var:iu_token = global.industry_base_elites_employment@var:iu_token }
			}
			else_if = { #Industrialized
				limit = {
					check_variable = { production_method@var:iu_token = 1 }
				}
				set_variable = { laborers_jobs@var:iu_token = global.industry_industrialized_laborers_employment@var:iu_token }
				set_variable = { workers_jobs@var:iu_token = global.industry_industrialized_workers_employment@var:iu_token }
				set_variable = { professionals_jobs@var:iu_token = global.industry_industrialized_professionals_employment@var:iu_token }
				set_variable = { elites_jobs@var:iu_token = global.industry_industrialized_elites_employment@var:iu_token }
			}
			else_if = { #Mechanized
				limit = {
					check_variable = { production_method@var:iu_token = 2 }
				}
				set_variable = { laborers_jobs@var:iu_token = global.industry_mechanized_laborers_employment@var:iu_token }
				set_variable = { workers_jobs@var:iu_token = global.industry_mechanized_workers_employment@var:iu_token }
				set_variable = { professionals_jobs@var:iu_token = global.industry_mechanized_professionals_employment@var:iu_token }
				set_variable = { elites_jobs@var:iu_token = global.industry_mechanized_elites_employment@var:iu_token }
			}
			else_if = { #Modernized
				limit = {
					check_variable = { production_method@var:iu_token = 3 }
				}
				set_variable = { laborers_jobs@var:iu_token = global.industry_modernized_laborers_employment@var:iu_token }
				set_variable = { workers_jobs@var:iu_token = global.industry_modernized_workers_employment@var:iu_token }
				set_variable = { professionals_jobs@var:iu_token = global.industry_modernized_professionals_employment@var:iu_token }
				set_variable = { elites_jobs@var:iu_token = global.industry_modernized_elites_employment@var:iu_token }
			}
			multiply_variable = { laborers_jobs@var:iu_token = size@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { workers_jobs@var:iu_token =  size@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { professionals_jobs@var:iu_token = size@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { elites_jobs@var:iu_token =  size@var:iu_token }


			set_variable = { jobs@var:iu_token = laborers_jobs@var:iu_token }
			add_to_variable = { jobs@var:iu_token = workers_jobs@var:iu_token }
			add_to_variable = { jobs@var:iu_token = professionals_jobs@var:iu_token }
			add_to_variable = { jobs@var:iu_token = elites_jobs@var:iu_token }
		#
		#Employees Amount
			set_variable = { employed@var:iu_token = laborers_employed@var:iu_token }
			add_to_variable = { employed@var:iu_token = workers_employed@var:iu_token }
			add_to_variable = { employed@var:iu_token = professionals_employed@var:iu_token }
			add_to_variable = { employed@var:iu_token = elites_employed@var:iu_token }
		#
		
		#Employment Percentage
			set_variable = { employment_percentage@var:iu_token = employed@var:iu_token }
			divide_variable = { employment_percentage@var:iu_token = jobs@var:iu_token }
		#

		#Open Jobs
			set_temp_variable = { target_temp = employment_target@var:iu_token }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { target_temp = employment_percentage@var:iu_token }

			set_variable = { laborers_open_jobs@var:iu_token = laborers_jobs@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { laborers_open_jobs@var:iu_token = target_temp }
			set_variable = { workers_open_jobs@var:iu_token = workers_jobs@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { workers_open_jobs@var:iu_token = target_temp }
			set_variable = { professionals_open_jobs@var:iu_token = professionals_jobs@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { professionals_open_jobs@var:iu_token = target_temp }
			set_variable = { elites_open_jobs@var:iu_token = elites_jobs@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { elites_open_jobs@var:iu_token = target_temp }
		#
	}
	industry_update_production = {
		#iu_token

		#Production Percentage
			set_variable = { production_percentage@var:iu_token = employment_percentage@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { production_percentage@var:iu_token = 100 }
		#

		#Production Modifiers
			set_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = output_factor@var:iu_token }
			add_to_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = 1 }

			set_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = throughput_factor@var:iu_token }
			add_to_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = 1 }

			set_temp_variable = { input_modifier_temp = input_factor@var:iu_token }
			add_to_temp_variable = { input_modifier_temp = 1 }

			set_temp_variable = { maintenance_modifier_temp = maintenance_factor@var:iu_token }
			add_to_temp_variable = { maintenance_modifier_temp = 1 }
		#

		#Max Production
			set_variable = { max_production@var:iu_token = size@var:iu_token }
			if = { #Base
				limit = {
					check_variable = { production_method@var:iu_token = 0 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { max_production_temp = global.industry_base_output@var:iu_token }
			}
			else_if = { #Industrialized
				limit = {

					multiply_variable = { maintenance_6_amount@var:iu_token = throughput_modifier_temp }
					multiply_variable = { maintenance_6_amount@var:iu_token = maintenance_modifier_temp }
				}
				else_if = { #Modernized
					limit = {
						check_variable = { production_method@var:iu_token = 3 }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { maintenance_r = global.industry_modernized_maintenance_resource_1@var:iu_token }
					set_variable = { maintenance_1_amount@var:iu_token = global.industry_modernized_maintenance_amount_1@var:iu_token }
					multiply_variable = { maintenance_1_amount@var:iu_token = size@var:iu_token }
					multiply_variable = { maintenance_1_amount@var:iu_token = throughput_modifier_temp }
					multiply_variable = { maintenance_1_amount@var:iu_token = maintenance_modifier_temp }
					
					set_temp_variable = { maintenance_r = global.industry_modernized_maintenance_resource_2@var:iu_token }

					multiply_variable = { maintenance_2_amount@var:iu_token = throughput_modifier_temp }

					multiply_variable = { maintenance_6_amount@var:iu_token = size@var:iu_token }
					multiply_variable = { maintenance_6_amount@var:iu_token = throughput_modifier_temp }
					multiply_variable = { maintenance_6_amount@var:iu_token = maintenance_modifier_temp }
				}

				set_variable = { max_maintenance_1_amount@var:iu_token = maintenance_1_amount@var:iu_token }
				set_variable = { max_maintenance_2_amount@var:iu_token = maintenance_2_amount@var:iu_token }
				set_variable = { max_maintenance_3_amount@var:iu_token = maintenance_3_amount@var:iu_token }
				set_variable = { max_maintenance_4_amount@var:iu_token = maintenance_4_amount@var:iu_token }
				set_variable = { max_maintenance_5_amount@var:iu_token = maintenance_5_amount@var:iu_token }
				set_variable = { max_maintenance_6_amount@var:iu_token = maintenance_6_amount@var:iu_token }

				multiply_variable = { maintenance_1_amount@var:iu_token = production_percentage@var:iu_token }
				divide_variable = { maintenance_1_amount@var:iu_token = 100 }
				multiply_variable = { maintenance_2_amount@var:iu_token = production_percentage@var:iu_token }
				divide_variable = { maintenance_2_amount@var:iu_token = 100 }
				multiply_variable = { maintenance_3_amount@var:iu_token = production_percentage@var:iu_token }
				divide_variable = { maintenance_3_amount@var:iu_token = 100 }
				multiply_variable = { maintenance_4_amount@var:iu_token = production_percentage@var:iu_token }
				divide_variable = { maintenance_4_amount@var:iu_token = 100 }
				multiply_variable = { maintenance_5_amount@var:iu_token = production_percentage@var:iu_token }
				divide_variable = { maintenance_5_amount@var:iu_token = 100 }
				multiply_variable = { maintenance_6_amount@var:iu_token = production_percentage@var:iu_token }
				divide_variable = { maintenance_6_amount@var:iu_token = 100 }
			#
		#
		
		#Production
			set_variable = { production@var:iu_token = max_production@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { production@var:iu_token = production_percentage@var:iu_token }
			divide_variable = { production@var:iu_token = 100 }
		#
	}
	industry_update_finances = {
		#iu_token

		# Vars
			set_temp_variable = { iu_resource = global.industry_resource_output@var:iu_token }
			if = { #Base
				limit = {
					check_variable = { production_method@var:iu_token = 0 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { input_1_r = global.industry_base_input_resource_1@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { input_2_r = global.industry_base_input_resource_2@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { input_3_r = global.industry_base_input_resource_3@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { input_4_r = global.industry_base_input_resource_4@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { input_5_r = global.industry_base_input_resource_5@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { input_6_r = global.industry_base_input_resource_6@var:iu_token }

				set_temp_variable = { maintenance_1_r = global.industry_base_maintenance_resource_1@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { maintenance_2_r = global.industry_base_maintenance_resource_2@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { maintenance_3_r = global.industry_base_maintenance_resource_3@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { maintenance_4_r = global.industry_base_maintenance_resource_4@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { maintenance_5_r = global.industry_base_maintenance_resource_5@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { maintenance_6_r = global.industry_base_maintenance_resource_6@var:iu_token }
			}
			else_if = { #Industrialized
				limit = {
					check_variable = { production_method@var:iu_token = 1 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { input_1_r = global.industry_industrialized_input_resource_1@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { input_2_r = global.industry_industrialized_input_resource_2@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { input_3_r = global.industry_industrialized_input_resource_3@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { input_4_r = global.industry_industrialized_input_resource_4@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { input_5_r = global.industry_industrialized_input_resource_5@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { input_6_r = global.industry_industrialized_input_resource_6@var:iu_token }

				set_temp_variable = { maintenance_1_r = global.industry_industrialized_maintenance_resource_1@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { maintenance_2_r = global.industry_industrialized_maintenance_resource_2@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { maintenance_3_r = global.industry_industrialized_maintenance_resource_3@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { maintenance_4_r = global.industry_industrialized_maintenance_resource_4@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { maintenance_5_r = global.industry_industrialized_maintenance_resource_5@var:iu_token }

			else_if = { #Mechanized
				limit = {

				set_temp_variable = { input_1_r = global.industry_mechanized_input_resource_1@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { input_2_r = global.industry_mechanized_input_resource_2@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { input_3_r = global.industry_mechanized_input_resource_3@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { input_4_r = global.industry_mechanized_input_resource_4@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { input_5_r = global.industry_mechanized_input_resource_5@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { input_6_r = global.industry_mechanized_input_resource_6@var:iu_token }

				set_temp_variable = { maintenance_1_r = global.industry_mechanized_maintenance_resource_1@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { maintenance_2_r = global.industry_mechanized_maintenance_resource_2@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { maintenance_3_r = global.industry_mechanized_maintenance_resource_3@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { maintenance_4_r = global.industry_mechanized_maintenance_resource_4@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { maintenance_5_r = global.industry_mechanized_maintenance_resource_5@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { maintenance_6_r = global.industry_mechanized_maintenance_resource_6@var:iu_token }
			}
			else_if = { #Modernized
				limit = {
					check_variable = { production_method@var:iu_token = 3 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { input_1_r = global.industry_modernized_input_resource_1@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { input_2_r = global.industry_modernized_input_resource_2@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { input_3_r = global.industry_modernized_input_resource_3@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { input_4_r = global.industry_modernized_input_resource_4@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { input_5_r = global.industry_modernized_input_resource_5@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { input_6_r = global.industry_modernized_input_resource_6@var:iu_token }

				set_temp_variable = { maintenance_1_r = global.industry_modernized_maintenance_resource_1@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { maintenance_2_r = global.industry_modernized_maintenance_resource_2@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { maintenance_3_r = global.industry_modernized_maintenance_resource_3@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { maintenance_4_r = global.industry_modernized_maintenance_resource_4@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { maintenance_5_r = global.industry_modernized_maintenance_resource_5@var:iu_token }
				set_temp_variable = { maintenance_6_r = global.industry_modernized_maintenance_resource_6@var:iu_token }
			}
		#

		#Money Limit
			set_variable = { money_limit@var:iu_token = global.industry_money_limit }
			multiply_variable = { money_limit@var:iu_token = global.base_price@var:iu_resource }
			multiply_variable = { money_limit@var:iu_token = max_production@var:iu_token }
		#

		#Wages & Payroll
			#Wages
			set_variable = { laborers_payroll@var:iu_token = laborers_wage }
			multiply_variable = { laborers_payroll@var:iu_token = laborers_employed@var:iu_token }
			
			set_variable = { workers_payroll@var:iu_token = workers_wage }
			multiply_variable = { workers_payroll@var:iu_token = workers_employed@var:iu_token }
			
			set_variable = { professionals_payroll@var:iu_token = professionals_wage }
			multiply_variable = { professionals_payroll@var:iu_token = professionals_employed@var:iu_token }
			
			set_variable = { elites_payroll@var:iu_token = elites_wage }
			multiply_variable = { elites_payroll@var:iu_token = elites_employed@var:iu_token }
			
			#Payroll
			set_variable = { expenses_payroll@var:iu_token = laborers_payroll@var:iu_token }
			add_to_variable = { expenses_payroll@var:iu_token = workers_payroll@var:iu_token }
			add_to_variable = { expenses_payroll@var:iu_token = professionals_payroll@var:iu_token }
			add_to_variable = { expenses_payroll@var:iu_token = elites_payroll@var:iu_token }

			#Avg Wage
			set_variable = { average_wage@var:iu_token = expenses_payroll@var:iu_token }
			divide_variable = { average_wage@var:iu_token = employed@var:iu_token }
		#
		
		#Profit, Profitability, Revenue & Expenses

			#Revenue
			set_variable = { revenue_goods@var:iu_token = production@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { revenue_goods@var:iu_token = price@var:iu_resource }

			set_variable = { revenue@var:iu_token = revenue_goods@var:iu_token }

			#Expenses
			set_variable = { input_1_expenses@var:iu_token = input_1_amount@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { input_1_expenses@var:iu_token = price@var:input_1_r }
			set_variable = { input_2_expenses@var:iu_token = input_2_amount@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { input_2_expenses@var:iu_token = price@var:input_2_r }
			set_variable = { input_3_expenses@var:iu_token = input_3_amount@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { input_3_expenses@var:iu_token = price@var:input_3_r }
			set_variable = { input_4_expenses@var:iu_token = input_4_amount@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { input_4_expenses@var:iu_token = price@var:input_4_r }
			set_variable = { input_5_expenses@var:iu_token = input_5_amount@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { input_5_expenses@var:iu_token = price@var:input_5_r }
			set_variable = { input_6_expenses@var:iu_token = input_6_amount@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { input_6_expenses@var:iu_token = price@var:input_6_r }

			set_variable = { expenses_input@var:iu_token = input_1_expenses@var:iu_token }
			add_to_variable = { expenses_input@var:iu_token = input_2_expenses@var:iu_token }
			add_to_variable = { expenses_input@var:iu_token = input_3_expenses@var:iu_token }
			add_to_variable = { expenses_input@var:iu_token = input_4_expenses@var:iu_token }
			add_to_variable = { expenses_input@var:iu_token = input_5_expenses@var:iu_token }
			add_to_variable = { expenses_input@var:iu_token = input_6_expenses@var:iu_token }

			set_variable = { maintenance_1_expenses@var:iu_token = maintenance_1_amount@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { maintenance_1_expenses@var:iu_token = price@var:maintenance_1_r }
			set_variable = { maintenance_2_expenses@var:iu_token = maintenance_2_amount@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { maintenance_2_expenses@var:iu_token = price@var:maintenance_2_r }
			set_variable = { maintenance_3_expenses@var:iu_token = maintenance_3_amount@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { maintenance_3_expenses@var:iu_token = price@var:maintenance_3_r }
			set_variable = { maintenance_4_expenses@var:iu_token = maintenance_4_amount@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { maintenance_4_expenses@var:iu_token = price@var:maintenance_4_r }
			set_variable = { maintenance_5_expenses@var:iu_token = maintenance_5_amount@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { maintenance_5_expenses@var:iu_token = price@var:maintenance_5_r }
			set_variable = { maintenance_6_expenses@var:iu_token = maintenance_6_amount@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { maintenance_6_expenses@var:iu_token = price@var:maintenance_6_r }

			set_variable = { expenses_maintenance@var:iu_token = maintenance_1_expenses@var:iu_token }
			add_to_variable = { expenses_maintenance@var:iu_token = maintenance_2_expenses@var:iu_token }
			add_to_variable = { expenses_maintenance@var:iu_token = maintenance_3_expenses@var:iu_token }
			add_to_variable = { expenses_maintenance@var:iu_token = maintenance_4_expenses@var:iu_token }
			add_to_variable = { expenses_maintenance@var:iu_token = maintenance_5_expenses@var:iu_token }
			add_to_variable = { expenses_maintenance@var:iu_token = maintenance_6_expenses@var:iu_token }
			add_to_variable = { expenses_maintenance@var:iu_token = maintenance_7_expenses@var:iu_token }
			add_to_variable = { expenses_maintenance@var:iu_token = maintenance_8_expenses@var:iu_token }

			set_variable = { expenses@var:iu_token = expenses_payroll@var:iu_token }
			add_to_variable = { expenses@var:iu_token = expenses_input@var:iu_token }
			add_to_variable = { expenses@var:iu_token = expenses_maintenance@var:iu_token }

			#Profit
			set_variable = { profit@var:iu_token = revenue@var:iu_token }
			subtract_from_variable = { profit@var:iu_token = expenses@var:iu_token }

			#Subsidies
			set_variable = { revenue_subsidies@var:iu_token = 0 }
			if = { #Keep Afloat
				limit = {
					check_variable = { subsidy@var:iu_token = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { profit@var:iu_token < 0 }
					}
					set_variable = { revenue_subsidies@var:iu_token = profit@var:iu_token }
					multiply_variable = { revenue_subsidies@var:iu_token = -1 }
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Subsidize Output
				limit = {
					check_variable = { subsidy@var:iu_token = 2 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { profit@var:iu_token < 0 }
					}
					set_variable = { revenue_subsidies@var:iu_token = profit@var:iu_token }
					multiply_variable = { revenue_subsidies@var:iu_token = -1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { expenses_maintenance@var:iu_token > revenue_subsidies@var:iu_token }
					}
					set_variable = { revenue_subsidies@var:iu_token = expenses_maintenance@var:iu_token }
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Bankroll
				limit = {
					check_variable = { subsidy@var:iu_token = 3 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { profit@var:iu_token < 0 }
					}
					set_variable = { revenue_subsidies@var:iu_token = profit@var:iu_token }
					multiply_variable = { revenue_subsidies@var:iu_token = -1 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { subsidy_temp = expenses_input@var:iu_token }
				add_to_temp_variable = { subsidy_temp = expenses_maintenance@var:iu_token }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { subsidy_temp > revenue_subsidies@var:iu_token }
					}
					set_variable = { revenue_subsidies@var:iu_token = subsidy_temp }
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { revenue@var:iu_token = revenue_subsidies@var:iu_token }
			add_to_variable = { profit@var:iu_token = revenue_subsidies@var:iu_token }

			#Bonuses
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { profit@var:iu_token > 0 }
				}
				set_variable = { expenses_bonuses@var:iu_token = profit@var:iu_token }
				multiply_variable = { expenses_bonuses@var:iu_token = global.industry_bonuses_percentage }
				add_to_variable = { expenses@var:iu_token = expenses_bonuses@var:iu_token }
				subtract_from_variable = { profit@var:iu_token = expenses_bonuses@var:iu_token }
				
				set_variable = { laborers_bonuses@var:iu_token = expenses_bonuses@var:iu_token }
				multiply_variable = { laborers_bonuses@var:iu_token = laborers_wage@var:iu_token }
				multiply_variable = { laborers_bonuses@var:iu_token = laborers_employed@var:iu_token }
				divide_variable = { laborers_bonuses@var:iu_token = average_wage@var:iu_token }
				divide_variable = { laborers_bonuses@var:iu_token = employed@var:iu_token }
				
				set_variable = { workers_bonuses@var:iu_token = expenses_bonuses@var:iu_token }
				multiply_variable = { workers_bonuses@var:iu_token = workers_wage@var:iu_token }
				multiply_variable = { workers_bonuses@var:iu_token = workers_employed@var:iu_token }
				divide_variable = { workers_bonuses@var:iu_token = average_wage@var:iu_token }
				divide_variable = { workers_bonuses@var:iu_token = employed@var:iu_token }
				
				set_variable = { professionals_bonuses@var:iu_token = expenses_bonuses@var:iu_token }
				multiply_variable = { professionals_bonuses@var:iu_token = professionals_wage@var:iu_token }
				multiply_variable = { professionals_bonuses@var:iu_token = professionals_employed@var:iu_token }
				divide_variable = { professionals_bonuses@var:iu_token = average_wage@var:iu_token }
				divide_variable = { professionals_bonuses@var:iu_token = employed@var:iu_token }
				
				set_variable = { elites_bonuses@var:iu_token = expenses_bonuses@var:iu_token }
				multiply_variable = { elites_bonuses@var:iu_token = elites_wage@var:iu_token }
				multiply_variable = { elites_bonuses@var:iu_token = elites_employed@var:iu_token }
				divide_variable = { elites_bonuses@var:iu_token = average_wage@var:iu_token }
				divide_variable = { elites_bonuses@var:iu_token = employed@var:iu_token }
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = { expenses_bonuses@var:iu_token = 0 }
				set_variable = { laborers_bonuses@var:iu_token = 0 }
				set_variable = { workers_bonuses@var:iu_token = 0 }
				set_variable = { professionals_bonuses@var:iu_token = 0 }
				set_variable = { elites_bonuses@var:iu_token = 0 }
			}

			#Profitability
			set_variable = { profitability@var:iu_token = profit@var:iu_token }
			divide_variable = { profitability@var:iu_token = revenue@var:iu_token }
		#

		#Productivity
            set_temp_variable = { revenue_temp = max_production@var:iu_token }
            multiply_temp_variable = { revenue_temp = price@var:iu_resource }
			
			set_variable = { max_input_1_expenses@var:iu_token = max_input_1_amount@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { max_input_1_expenses@var:iu_token = price@var:input_1_r }
			set_variable = { max_input_2_expenses@var:iu_token = max_input_2_amount@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { max_input_2_expenses@var:iu_token = price@var:input_2_r }
			set_variable = { max_input_3_expenses@var:iu_token = max_input_3_amount@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { max_input_3_expenses@var:iu_token = price@var:input_3_r }
			set_variable = { max_input_4_expenses@var:iu_token = max_input_4_amount@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { max_input_4_expenses@var:iu_token = price@var:input_4_r }
			set_variable = { max_input_5_expenses@var:iu_token = max_input_5_amount@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { max_input_5_expenses@var:iu_token = price@var:input_5_r }
			set_variable = { max_input_6_expenses@var:iu_token = max_input_6_amount@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { max_input_6_expenses@var:iu_token = price@var:input_6_r }

			set_variable = { max_maintenance_1_expenses@var:iu_token = max_maintenance_1_amount@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { max_maintenance_1_expenses@var:iu_token = price@var:maintenance_1_r }
			set_variable = { max_maintenance_2_expenses@var:iu_token = max_maintenance_2_amount@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { max_maintenance_2_expenses@var:iu_token = price@var:maintenance_2_r }
			set_variable = { max_maintenance_3_expenses@var:iu_token = max_maintenance_3_amount@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { max_maintenance_3_expenses@var:iu_token = price@var:maintenance_3_r }
			set_variable = { max_maintenance_4_expenses@var:iu_token = max_maintenance_4_amount@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { max_maintenance_4_expenses@var:iu_token = price@var:maintenance_4_r }
			set_variable = { max_maintenance_5_expenses@var:iu_token = max_maintenance_5_amount@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { max_maintenance_5_expenses@var:iu_token = price@var:maintenance_5_r }
			set_variable = { max_maintenance_6_expenses@var:iu_token = max_maintenance_6_amount@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { max_maintenance_6_expenses@var:iu_token = price@var:maintenance_6_r }
            
            set_temp_variable = { expenses_temp = 0 }
            add_to_temp_variable = { expenses_temp = max_input_1_expenses@var:iu_token }
            add_to_temp_variable = { expenses_temp = max_input_2_expenses@var:iu_token }
            add_to_temp_variable = { expenses_temp = max_input_3_expenses@var:iu_token }
            add_to_temp_variable = { expenses_temp = max_input_4_expenses@var:iu_token }
            add_to_temp_variable = { expenses_temp = max_input_5_expenses@var:iu_token }
            add_to_temp_variable = { expenses_temp = max_input_6_expenses@var:iu_token }
            add_to_temp_variable = { expenses_temp = max_maintenance_1_expenses@var:iu_token }
            add_to_temp_variable = { expenses_temp = max_maintenance_2_expenses@var:iu_token }
            add_to_temp_variable = { expenses_temp = max_maintenance_3_expenses@var:iu_token }
            add_to_temp_variable = { expenses_temp = max_maintenance_4_expenses@var:iu_token }
            add_to_temp_variable = { expenses_temp = max_maintenance_5_expenses@var:iu_token }
            add_to_temp_variable = { expenses_temp = max_maintenance_6_expenses@var:iu_token }

			set_variable = { productivity@var:iu_token = revenue_temp }
			subtract_from_variable = { productivity@var:iu_token = expenses_temp }

			#Base Productivity
			set_variable = { base_productivity@var:iu_token = productivity@var:iu_token }
			set_temp_variable = { jobs_weighted_temp = laborers_jobs@var:iu_token }
			multiply_temp_variable = { jobs_weighted_temp = 2 }
			
			set_temp_variable = { weighted_temp = workers_jobs@var:iu_token }
			multiply_temp_variable = { weighted_temp = 5 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { jobs_weighted_temp = weighted_temp }
			
			set_temp_variable = { weighted_temp = professionals_jobs@var:iu_token }
			multiply_temp_variable = { weighted_temp = 10 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { jobs_weighted_temp = weighted_temp }
			
			set_temp_variable = { weighted_temp = elites_jobs@var:iu_token }
			multiply_temp_variable = { weighted_temp = 25 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { jobs_weighted_temp = weighted_temp }

			divide_variable = { base_productivity@var:iu_token = jobs_weighted_temp }
			divide_variable = { productivity@var:iu_token = jobs@var:iu_token }
		#
	}

	industry_change_production_method = {
		#industry_token, #pm_num
		set_temp_variable = { iu_token = industry_token }

		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = { pm_num = 0 }
						NOT = { check_variable = { global.industry_base_tech_unlock@var:industry_token = -1 } }
					}
					AND = {
						check_variable = { pm_num = 1 }
						NOT = { check_variable = { global.industry_industrialized_tech_unlock@var:industry_token = -1 } }
					}
					AND = {
						check_variable = { pm_num = 2 }
						NOT = { check_variable = { global.industry_mechanized_tech_unlock@var:industry_token = -1 } }
					}
					AND = {
						check_variable = { pm_num = 3 }
						NOT = { check_variable = { global.industry_modernized_tech_unlock@var:industry_token = -1 } }
					}
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { emp_percent_temp = employment_percentage@var:industry_token }
			set_variable = { production_method@var:industry_token = pm_num }

			#Fires everyone then rehires everyone basically.
			set_variable = { employment_percentage@var:industry_token = 0 }
			subtract_from_variable = { laborers_employed_amount = laborers_employed@var:industry_token }
			subtract_from_variable = { workers_employed_amount = workers_employed@var:industry_token }
			subtract_from_variable = { professionals_employed_amount = professionals_employed@var:industry_token }
			subtract_from_variable = { elites_employed_amount = elites_employed@var:industry_token }
			set_variable = { laborers_employed@var:industry_token = 0 }			
			set_variable = { workers_employed@var:industry_token = 0 }
			set_variable = { professionals_employed@var:industry_token = 0 }
			set_variable = { elites_employed@var:industry_token = 0 }

			industry_update_workforce = yes
			pops_update_workforce = yes

			log = "[?employment_percentage@var:industry_token]"
			
			set_temp_variable = { x_percent_temp = emp_percent_temp }
			set_industry_employment_to_x_percent = yes
			
			industry_update = yes
		}
	}

	industries_update_civ_count = {
		set_temp_variable = { civ_count = industrial_power }
		divide_temp_variable = { civ_count = global.industrial_complex_per_x }
		round_temp_variable = civ_count
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { building_level@industrial_complex = civ_count } }
			}
			meta_effect = {
				text = {
					set_building_level = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = [Industries_Num]
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				Industries_Num = "[?civ_count|0]"
			}
		}
	}
	industries_update_construction = {
		clear_array = industries_under_construction_array
		set_variable = { industries_under_construction_amount = 0 }
		for_each_loop = {
			array = industries
			value = om_industry

			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { under_construction@var:om_industry > 0 }
				}
				add_to_array = { industries_under_construction_array = om_industry }
				add_to_variable = { industries_under_construction_amount = under_construction@var:om_industry }

				set_temp_variable = { const_r = global.industry_base_construction_resource@var:om_industry }

				set_variable = { construction_speed@var:om_industry = global.industry_base_construction_speed@var:om_industry }
				multiply_variable = { construction_speed@var:om_industry = under_construction@var:om_industry }

				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { construction_speed@var:om_industry > construction_amount@var:om_industry }
					}
					set_variable = { construction_speed@var:om_industry = construction_amount@var:om_industry }
				}

				set_variable = { construction_expenses@var:om_industry = construction_speed@var:om_industry }
				multiply_variable = { construction_expenses@var:om_industry = price@var:const_r }
			}
		}
	}
	
	industries_base_attractiveness_calc = {
		#COUNTRY SCOPE

		# This is the base willingness for the AI to invest in each industry
		# AI will only consider state industries that are > 0 attractiveness nationally (which are added into a list)
		#
		# AI will then go through each state and only consider building industries > 100 attractiveness

		# Note: 
		#   IE is short for Ingame Effect, not an example
		#
		# Investment:
		#   Things that affect the likelyhood to build/expand an industry:
		#		= Rate of Return
		#			IE - Using Profitability & Productivity and dividing that by construction cost
		#       = Existing buildings VS new sites
		#           IE - Building new industries in a new state has a much higher bar for attractiveness
		#		= Availability of Capital
		#			IE - Local Elites & Corporations having a lot of money to expand industry will make them more likely to invest
		#       = Financial Incentives/Disincentives
		#           IE - Private Investors will take into account the following:
		#               +  Industrial Subsidies (if applied to the industry)
		#               -  Taxation (Corporate/Income/Sales/Tariffs)
		#       = Infrastructure
		#           IE - Infrastructure capacity in state
		#       = Labor Availability
		#           IE - Less profitable industries will be significantly less attractive
		#		= Labor Quality
		#			IE - If not enough qualified labor, then significantly less attractive
		#       = National/Global Status
		#           IE - Different laws & values & modifiers affect investment confidence
		#               + Investment Confidence (Adds onto attractiveness)
		#                   +  Pro-Growth Govt. Policy
		#					-  Anti-Growth Govt. Policy
		#                   +  High Stability
		#                   -- Low Stability (REALLY BAD. Businesses want stability)
		#                   +  National GDP Growth
		#                   +  National Inflation (Inflation means money is better spent today)
		#                   -  National Deflation (Deflation means money is better saved)
		#                   +  National Population Growth
		#                   +- Events, Ideas, & Focuses 
		
		clear_array = attractive_industries_array
		for_each_loop = {
			array = global.industries_token_array
			value = iu_token
			index = ind
			break = ind_break

			industry_potential_calc = yes
			
			#Return Rate
			set_variable = { attractiveness@var:iu_token = potential_profit@var:iu_token }
			multiply_variable = { attractiveness@var:iu_token = global.ai_profit_return }
			multiply_variable = { attractiveness@var:iu_token = 12 }

			set_temp_variable = { const_r = global.industry_base_construction_resource@var:iu_token }
			set_temp_variable = { const_cost = global.industry_base_construction_amount@var:iu_token }
			multiply_temp_variable = { const_cost = price@var:const_r }
			divide_variable = { attractiveness@var:iu_token = const_cost }
			multiply_variable = { attractiveness@var:iu_token = global.ai_return_rate_attractiveness_factor }

			#Labor Quality
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { potential_workers > 0 }
					}
					#TODO - Check for literacy
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { potential_professionals > 0 }
					}
					#TODO - Check for literacy
				}
			#

			#Attractiveness Modifier & Factor
			add_to_variable = { attractiveness@var:iu_token = attractiveness_modifier@var:iu_token }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier_temp = attractiveness_factor@var:iu_token }
			add_to_temp_variable = { modifier_temp = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { attractiveness@var:iu_token > 0 }
				}
				multiply_variable = { attractiveness@var:iu_token = modifier_temp }
				add_to_array = { attractive_industries_array = iu_token }
				
				#State-wide Attractiveness
				every_controlled_state = {
					calc_local_attractiveness = yes
				}
			}
			else = {
				every_controlled_state = {
					set_variable = { attractiveness@var:iu_token = 0 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	industry_potential_calc = {
		#iu_token
		#Country Scope

		# potential_profit
		# potential_productivity
		# potential_laborers
		# potential_workers
		# potential_professionals
		# potential_elites
		# potential_jobs
		
		set_temp_variable = { iu_resource = global.industry_resource_output@var:iu_token }
		set_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = output_factor@var:iu_token }
		add_to_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = 1 }

		set_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = throughput_factor@var:iu_token }
		add_to_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = 1 }

		set_temp_variable = { input_modifier_temp = input_factor@var:iu_token }
		add_to_temp_variable = { input_modifier_temp = 1 }

		set_temp_variable = { maintenance_modifier_temp = maintenance_factor@var:iu_token }
		add_to_temp_variable = { maintenance_modifier_temp = 1 }

		#Modernized
		if = {
			limit = {
				set_temp_variable = { tech_temp = global.industry_modernized_tech_unlock@var:iu_token }
				NOT = { check_variable = { tech_temp = -1 } }
				OR = {
					check_variable = { tech_temp = 0 }
					has_tech = var:tech_temp
				}
			}

			#Revenue
			set_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = price@var:iu_resource }
			multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = global.industry_modernized_output@var:iu_token }
			multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = output_modifier_temp }
			multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = throughput_modifier_temp }

			#Expenses
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { global.industry_modernized_input_amount_1@var:iu_token > 0 }
				}

				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = input_modifier_temp }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = ipc_exp }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { global.industry_modernized_input_amount_2@var:iu_token > 0 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { ipc_imr = global.industry_modernized_input_resource_2@var:iu_token }

				set_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = global.industry_modernized_input_amount_2@var:iu_token }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = price@var:ipc_imr }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = input_modifier_temp }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = ipc_exp }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { global.industry_modernized_input_amount_3@var:iu_token > 0 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { ipc_imr = global.industry_modernized_input_resource_3@var:iu_token }

				set_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = global.industry_modernized_input_amount_3@var:iu_token }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = price@var:ipc_imr }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = input_modifier_temp }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = ipc_exp }
			}
			if = {

				}
				set_temp_variable = { ipc_imr = global.industry_modernized_input_resource_4@var:iu_token }

				set_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = global.industry_modernized_input_amount_4@var:iu_token }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = price@var:ipc_imr }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = input_modifier_temp }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = ipc_exp }
			}

				}
				set_temp_variable = { ipc_imr = global.industry_modernized_input_resource_5@var:iu_token }

				set_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = global.industry_modernized_input_amount_5@var:iu_token }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = price@var:ipc_imr }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = input_modifier_temp }

			multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = 5 }

				set_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = global.industry_industrialized_maintenance_amount_8@var:iu_token }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = price@var:ipc_imr }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = maintenance_modifier_temp }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = ipc_exp }
			}

			set_variable = { potential_productivity@var:iu_token = ipc_profit }
			
			set_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = global.industry_industrialized_laborers_employment@var:iu_token }
			multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = 2 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = base_wage }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = ipc_exp }
			
			set_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = global.industry_industrialized_workers_employment@var:iu_token }
			multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = 5 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = base_wage }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = ipc_exp }
			
			set_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = global.industry_industrialized_professionals_employment@var:iu_token }
			multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = 10 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = base_wage }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = ipc_exp }

			multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = 25 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = base_wage }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = ipc_exp }

			set_variable = { potential_profit@var:iu_token = ipc_profit }

			set_temp_variable = { ipc_employees = global.industry_industrialized_laborers_employment@var:iu_token }
			add_to_temp_variable = { ipc_employees = global.industry_industrialized_workers_employment@var:iu_token }
			add_to_temp_variable = { ipc_employees = global.industry_industrialized_professionals_employment@var:iu_token }
			add_to_temp_variable = { ipc_employees = global.industry_industrialized_elites_employment@var:iu_token }
			divide_variable = { potential_productivity@var:iu_token = ipc_employees }
			
			set_variable = { potential_laborers@var:iu_token = global.industry_industrialized_laborers_employment@var:iu_token }
			set_variable = { potential_workers@var:iu_token = global.industry_industrialized_workers_employment@var:iu_token }
			set_variable = { potential_professionals@var:iu_token = global.industry_industrialized_professionals_employment@var:iu_token }
			set_variable = { potential_elites@var:iu_token = global.industry_industrialized_elites_employment@var:iu_token }
			set_variable = { potential_jobs@var:iu_token = ipc_employees }
		}
		#Base
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				set_temp_variable = { tech_temp = global.industry_base_tech_unlock@var:iu_token }
				NOT = { check_variable = { tech_temp = -1 } }
				OR = {
					check_variable = { tech_temp = 0 }
					has_tech = var:tech_temp
				}
			}

			#Revenue
			set_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = price@var:iu_resource }
			multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = global.industry_base_output@var:iu_token }
			multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = output_modifier_temp }
			multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = throughput_modifier_temp }

			#Expenses
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { global.industry_base_input_amount_1@var:iu_token > 0 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { ipc_imr = global.industry_base_input_resource_1@var:iu_token }

				set_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = global.industry_base_input_amount_1@var:iu_token }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = price@var:ipc_imr }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = input_modifier_temp }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = ipc_exp }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { global.industry_base_input_amount_2@var:iu_token > 0 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { ipc_imr = global.industry_base_input_resource_2@var:iu_token }

				set_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = global.industry_base_input_amount_2@var:iu_token }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = price@var:ipc_imr }

				set_temp_variable = { ipc_imr = global.industry_base_input_resource_4@var:iu_token }

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = ipc_exp }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { global.industry_base_input_amount_6@var:iu_token > 0 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { ipc_imr = global.industry_base_input_resource_6@var:iu_token }

				set_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = global.industry_base_input_amount_6@var:iu_token }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = price@var:ipc_imr }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = input_modifier_temp }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = ipc_exp }

			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { global.industry_base_maintenance_amount_1@var:iu_token > 0 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { ipc_imr = global.industry_base_maintenance_resource_1@var:iu_token }

				set_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = global.industry_base_maintenance_amount_1@var:iu_token }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = price@var:ipc_imr }

				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }

				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = price@var:ipc_imr }

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = ipc_exp }

					check_variable = { global.industry_base_maintenance_amount_6@var:iu_token > 0 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { ipc_imr = global.industry_base_maintenance_resource_6@var:iu_token }

				set_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = global.industry_base_maintenance_amount_6@var:iu_token }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = price@var:ipc_imr }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = maintenance_modifier_temp }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = ipc_exp }

					check_variable = { global.industry_base_maintenance_amount_7@var:iu_token > 0 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { ipc_imr = global.industry_base_maintenance_resource_7@var:iu_token }

				set_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = global.industry_base_maintenance_amount_7@var:iu_token }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = price@var:ipc_imr }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = maintenance_modifier_temp }
				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = ipc_exp }

				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = price@var:ipc_imr }

				multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = ipc_exp }
			}

			set_variable = { potential_productivity@var:iu_token = ipc_profit }
			
			set_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = global.industry_base_laborers_employment@var:iu_token }
			multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = 2 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = base_wage }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = ipc_exp }
			
			set_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = global.industry_base_workers_employment@var:iu_token }
			multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = 5 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = base_wage }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = ipc_exp }
			
			set_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = global.industry_base_professionals_employment@var:iu_token }
			multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = 10 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = base_wage }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = ipc_exp }
			
			set_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = global.industry_base_elites_employment@var:iu_token }
			multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = 25 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { ipc_exp = base_wage }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { ipc_profit = ipc_exp }

			set_variable = { potential_profit@var:iu_token = ipc_profit }

			set_temp_variable = { ipc_employees = global.industry_base_laborers_employment@var:iu_token }
			add_to_temp_variable = { ipc_employees = global.industry_base_workers_employment@var:iu_token }
			add_to_temp_variable = { ipc_employees = global.industry_base_professionals_employment@var:iu_token }
			add_to_temp_variable = { ipc_employees = global.industry_base_elites_employment@var:iu_token }
			divide_variable = { potential_productivity@var:iu_token = ipc_employees }
			
			set_variable = { potential_laborers@var:iu_token = global.industry_base_laborers_employment@var:iu_token }
			set_variable = { potential_workers@var:iu_token = global.industry_base_workers_employment@var:iu_token }
			set_variable = { potential_professionals@var:iu_token = global.industry_base_professionals_employment@var:iu_token }
			set_variable = { potential_elites@var:iu_token = global.industry_base_elites_employment@var:iu_token }
			set_variable = { potential_jobs@var:iu_token = ipc_employees }
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = { potential_productivity@var:iu_token = 0 }
			set_variable = { potential_profit@var:iu_token = 0 }
			set_variable = { potential_laborers@var:iu_token = 0 }
			set_variable = { potential_workers@var:iu_token = 0 }
			set_variable = { potential_professionals@var:iu_token = 0 }
			set_variable = { potential_elites@var:iu_token = 0 }
			set_variable = { potential_jobs@var:iu_token = 0 }
		}
	}
	calc_local_attractiveness = {
		#iu_token
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { global.industry_uses_deposits@var:iu_token = 0 }
					AND = {
						check_variable = { global.industry_uses_deposits@var:iu_token = 1 }
						check_variable = { deposits@var:iu_token > size@var:iu_token }
					}
				}
				OR = {
					check_variable = { global.industry_uses_arable_land@var:iu_token = 0 }
					AND = {
						check_variable = { global.industry_uses_arable_land@var:iu_token = 1 }
						check_variable = { arable_land > arable_land_used }
					}
				}
				OR = {
					check_variable = { global.industry_coastal@var:clist_token = 0 }
					AND = {
						check_variable = { global.industry_coastal@var:clist_token = 1 }
						var:selected_state = {
							is_coastal = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}

			#Return Rate
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { size@var:iu_token = 0 }
				}
				industry_potential_calc = yes
				set_variable = { attractiveness@var:iu_token = potential_profit@var:iu_token }
				multiply_variable = { attractiveness@var:iu_token = global.ai_profit_return }
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = { attractiveness@var:iu_token = profit@var:iu_token }
				divide_variable = { attractiveness@var:iu_token = size@var:iu_token }
			}
			multiply_variable = { attractiveness@var:iu_token = 12 }

			set_temp_variable = { const_r = global.industry_base_construction_resource@var:iu_token }
			set_temp_variable = { const_cost = global.industry_base_construction_amount@var:iu_token }
			multiply_temp_variable = { const_cost = price@var:const_r }
			divide_variable = { attractiveness@var:iu_token = const_cost }
			multiply_variable = { attractiveness@var:iu_token = global.ai_return_rate_attractiveness_factor }

			#Labor Quality
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { potential_workers > 0 }
					}
					#TODO - Check for literacy
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { potential_professionals > 0 }
					}
					#TODO - Check for literacy
				}
			#

			#If no industry is there
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { size@var:iu_token = 0 }
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { attractiveness@var:iu_token = 100 }
			}

			#Less attractive if already being built in the nation
			set_temp_variable = { subtract_temp = controller:under_construction@var:iu_token }
			multiply_temp_variable = { subtract_temp = global.attractivenss_decrease_from_construction }
			subtract_from_variable = { attractiveness@var:iu_token = subtract_temp }

			#Attractiveness Modifier & Factor
			add_to_variable = { attractiveness@var:iu_token = local_attractiveness_modifier@var:iu_token }
			add_to_variable = { attractiveness@var:iu_token = PREV.attractiveness_modifier@var:iu_token }
			set_temp_variable = { modifier_temp = local_attractiveness_factor@var:iu_token }
			add_to_temp_variable = { modifier_temp = PREV.attractiveness_factor@var:iu_token }
			add_to_temp_variable = { modifier_temp = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { attractiveness@var:iu_token > 0 }
				}
				multiply_variable = { attractiveness@var:iu_token = modifier_temp }
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = { attractiveness@var:iu_token = 0 }
		}
	}

	arable_land_update = {
		set_variable = { arable_land_used = 0 }

		for_each_loop = {
			array = industries
			value = al_token
			index = ind
			break = ind_break
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { global.industry_uses_arable_land@var:al_token = 1 }
				}
				add_to_variable = { arable_land_used = size@var:al_token }
			}
		}

		set_variable = { arable_land_available = arable_land }
		subtract_from_variable = { arable_land_available = arable_land_used }
	}
