	subsistence_farm_update = {
		subsistence_farm_update_workforce = yes
		subsistence_farm_update_production = yes
		subsistence_farm_update_finances = yes
	}
	subsistence_farm_update_workforce = {
		#Jobs Amount
		set_variable = { peasants_jobs_subsistence_farm = global.subsistence_farms_base_peasants_employment }
		multiply_variable = { peasants_jobs_subsistence_farm = arable_land_available }

		set_variable = { elites_jobs_subsistence_farm = global.subsistence_farms_base_elites_employment }
		multiply_variable = { elites_jobs_subsistence_farm = arable_land_available }

		set_variable = { jobs_subsistence_farm = peasants_jobs_subsistence_farm }
		add_to_variable = { jobs_subsistence_farm = elites_jobs_subsistence_farm }
		
		#Employees Amount & Percentage
		set_variable = { employed_subsistence_farm = peasants_employed_subsistence_farm }
		add_to_variable = { employed_subsistence_farm = elites_employed_subsistence_farm }
		
		set_variable = { employment_percentage_subsistence_farm = employed_subsistence_farm }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { jobs_subsistence_farm > 1000 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { tvar = jobs_subsistence_farm }
			divide_temp_variable = { tvar = 100 }
			divide_variable = { employment_percentage_subsistence_farm = tvar }
		}
		else = {
			multiply_variable = { employment_percentage_subsistence_farm = 100 }
			divide_variable = { employment_percentage_subsistence_farm = jobs_subsistence_farm }
		}
	}
	subsistence_farm_update_production = {
		#Production Modifiers
			set_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = output_factor_subsistence_farm }
			add_to_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = 1 }
		#

		#Max Production
			set_variable = { max_foodstuffs_production_subsistence_farm = global.subsistence_farms_foodstuffs_output }
			multiply_variable = { max_foodstuffs_production_subsistence_farm = arable_land_available }
			multiply_variable = { max_foodstuffs_production_subsistence_farm = output_modifier_temp }
			
			set_variable = { max_housing_production_subsistence_farm = global.subsistence_farms_housing_output }
			multiply_variable = { max_housing_production_subsistence_farm = arable_land_available }
			multiply_variable = { max_housing_production_subsistence_farm = output_modifier_temp }

			set_variable = { max_lumber_production_subsistence_farm = global.subsistence_farms_lumber_output }
			multiply_variable = { max_lumber_production_subsistence_farm = arable_land_available }
			multiply_variable = { max_lumber_production_subsistence_farm = output_modifier_temp }

			set_variable = { max_fiber_production_subsistence_farm = global.subsistence_farms_fiber_output }
			multiply_variable = { max_fiber_production_subsistence_farm = arable_land_available }
			multiply_variable = { max_fiber_production_subsistence_farm = output_modifier_temp }

			set_variable = { max_fabric_production_subsistence_farm = global.subsistence_farms_fabric_output }
			multiply_variable = { max_fabric_production_subsistence_farm = arable_land_available }
			multiply_variable = { max_fabric_production_subsistence_farm = output_modifier_temp }
		#

		#Production
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { max_foodstuffs_production_subsistence_farm > 10000 }
				}
				set_variable = { foodstuffs_production_subsistence_farm = max_foodstuffs_production_subsistence_farm }
				divide_variable = { foodstuffs_production_subsistence_farm = 100 }
				multiply_variable = { foodstuffs_production_subsistence_farm = employment_percentage_subsistence_farm }
				
				set_variable = { housing_production_subsistence_farm = max_housing_production_subsistence_farm }
				divide_variable = { housing_production_subsistence_farm = 100 }
				multiply_variable = { housing_production_subsistence_farm = employment_percentage_subsistence_farm }
				
				set_variable = { lumber_production_subsistence_farm = max_lumber_production_subsistence_farm }
				divide_variable = { lumber_production_subsistence_farm = 100 }
				multiply_variable = { lumber_production_subsistence_farm = employment_percentage_subsistence_farm }
				
				set_variable = { fiber_production_subsistence_farm = max_fiber_production_subsistence_farm }
				divide_variable = { fiber_production_subsistence_farm = 100 }
				multiply_variable = { fiber_production_subsistence_farm = employment_percentage_subsistence_farm }
				
				set_variable = { fabric_production_subsistence_farm = max_fabric_production_subsistence_farm }
				divide_variable = { fabric_production_subsistence_farm = 100 }
				multiply_variable = { fabric_production_subsistence_farm = employment_percentage_subsistence_farm }
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = { foodstuffs_production_subsistence_farm = max_foodstuffs_production_subsistence_farm }
				multiply_variable = { foodstuffs_production_subsistence_farm = employment_percentage_subsistence_farm }
				divide_variable = { foodstuffs_production_subsistence_farm = 100 }
				
				set_variable = { housing_production_subsistence_farm = max_housing_production_subsistence_farm }
				multiply_variable = { housing_production_subsistence_farm = employment_percentage_subsistence_farm }
				divide_variable = { housing_production_subsistence_farm = 100 }
				
				set_variable = { lumber_production_subsistence_farm = max_lumber_production_subsistence_farm }
				multiply_variable = { lumber_production_subsistence_farm = employment_percentage_subsistence_farm }
				divide_variable = { lumber_production_subsistence_farm = 100 }

				set_variable = { fiber_production_subsistence_farm = max_fiber_production_subsistence_farm }
				multiply_variable = { fiber_production_subsistence_farm = employment_percentage_subsistence_farm }
				divide_variable = { fiber_production_subsistence_farm = 100 }
			
				set_variable = { fabric_production_subsistence_farm = max_fabric_production_subsistence_farm }
				multiply_variable = { fabric_production_subsistence_farm = employment_percentage_subsistence_farm }
				divide_variable = { fabric_production_subsistence_farm = 100 }
			}
		#
	}
	subsistence_farm_update_finances = {
		#Revenue
			set_variable = { revenue_subsistence_farm = 0 }

			set_variable = { revenue_foodstuffs_subsistence_farm = foodstuffs_production_subsistence_farm }
			multiply_variable = { revenue_foodstuffs_subsistence_farm = price@token:resource_foodstuffs }
			add_to_variable = { revenue_subsistence_farm = revenue_foodstuffs_subsistence_farm }
			
			set_variable = { revenue_housing_subsistence_farm = housing_production_subsistence_farm }
			multiply_variable = { revenue_housing_subsistence_farm = price@token:resource_housing }
			add_to_variable = { revenue_subsistence_farm = revenue_housing_subsistence_farm }
			
			set_variable = { revenue_lumber_subsistence_farm = lumber_production_subsistence_farm }
			multiply_variable = { revenue_lumber_subsistence_farm = price@token:resource_lumber }
			add_to_variable = { revenue_subsistence_farm = revenue_lumber_subsistence_farm }
			
			set_variable = { revenue_fiber_subsistence_farm = fiber_production_subsistence_farm }
			multiply_variable = { revenue_fiber_subsistence_farm = price@token:resource_fiber }
			add_to_variable = { revenue_subsistence_farm = revenue_fiber_subsistence_farm }
			
			set_variable = { revenue_fabric_subsistence_farm = fabric_production_subsistence_farm }
			multiply_variable = { revenue_fabric_subsistence_farm = price@token:resource_fabric }
			add_to_variable = { revenue_subsistence_farm = revenue_fabric_subsistence_farm }
		#

		#Wages & Payroll
			#Avg Wage
			set_variable = { average_wage_subsistence_farm = revenue_subsistence_farm }
			divide_variable = { average_wage_subsistence_farm = employed_subsistence_farm }

			set_temp_variable = { w_temp = elites_employed_subsistence_farm }
			multiply_temp_variable = { w_temp = 5 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { w_temp = peasants_employed_subsistence_farm }

			#Wages
			set_variable = { peasants_payroll_subsistence_farm = revenue_subsistence_farm }
			divide_variable = { peasants_payroll_subsistence_farm = w_temp }
			multiply_variable = { peasants_payroll_subsistence_farm = peasants_employed_subsistence_farm }

			set_variable = { peasants_wage_subsistence_farm = peasants_payroll_subsistence_farm }
			divide_variable = { peasants_wage_subsistence_farm = peasants_employed_subsistence_farm }
			

			set_variable = { elites_payroll_subsistence_farm = revenue_subsistence_farm }
			divide_variable = { elites_payroll_subsistence_farm = w_temp }
			multiply_variable = { elites_payroll_subsistence_farm = elites_employed_subsistence_farm }
			multiply_variable = { elites_payroll_subsistence_farm = 5 }
			
			set_variable = { elites_wage_subsistence_farm = elites_payroll_subsistence_farm }
			divide_variable = { elites_wage_subsistence_farm = elites_employed_subsistence_farm }
		#

		#Productivity
			set_variable = { productivity_subsistence_farm = revenue_subsistence_farm }
			divide_variable = { productivity_subsistence_farm = employed_subsistence_farm }
		#
	}
	
	market_capital_update = {
		# Country scope
		var:market_capital = {
			# Jobs
				set_variable = { jobs@token:market_capital = controller:trade_jobs }

				set_variable = { workers_jobs@token:market_capital = controller:trade_jobs }
				multiply_variable = { workers_jobs@token:market_capital = 0.9 }
				set_variable = { workers_open_jobs@token:market_capital = workers_jobs@token:market_capital }
				multiply_variable = { workers_open_jobs@token:market_capital = employment_target@token:market_capital }
				subtract_from_variable = { workers_open_jobs@token:market_capital = workers_employed@token:market_capital }

				set_variable = { elites_jobs@token:market_capital = controller:trade_jobs }
				subtract_from_variable = { elites_jobs@token:market_capital = workers_jobs@token:market_capital }
				set_variable = { elites_open_jobs@token:market_capital = elites_jobs@token:market_capital }
				multiply_variable = { elites_open_jobs@token:market_capital = employment_target@token:market_capital }
				subtract_from_variable = { elites_open_jobs@token:market_capital = elites_employed@token:market_capital }
			#
			set_variable = { money_limit@token:market_capital = controller:trade_jobs }
			multiply_variable = { money_limit@token:market_capital = 7 }

			# Payroll
				#Wages
				set_variable = { laborers_payroll@token:market_capital = laborers_wage }
				multiply_variable = { laborers_payroll@token:market_capital = laborers_employed@token:market_capital }
				
				set_variable = { workers_payroll@token:market_capital = workers_wage }
				multiply_variable = { workers_payroll@token:market_capital = workers_employed@token:market_capital }
				
				set_variable = { professionals_payroll@token:market_capital = professionals_wage }
				multiply_variable = { professionals_payroll@token:market_capital = professionals_employed@token:market_capital }
				
				set_variable = { elites_payroll@token:market_capital = elites_wage }
				multiply_variable = { elites_payroll@token:market_capital = elites_employed@token:market_capital }
				
				#Payroll
				set_variable = { expenses_payroll@token:market_capital = laborers_payroll@token:market_capital }
				add_to_variable = { expenses_payroll@token:market_capital = workers_payroll@token:market_capital }
				add_to_variable = { expenses_payroll@token:market_capital = professionals_payroll@token:market_capital }
				add_to_variable = { expenses_payroll@token:market_capital = elites_payroll@token:market_capital }

				#Avg Wage
				set_variable = { average_wage@token:market_capital = expenses_payroll@token:market_capital }
				divide_variable = { average_wage@token:market_capital = employed@token:market_capital }
			#
			set_variable = { profit@token:market_capital = controller:trade_profit }
			subtract_from_variable = { profit@token:market_capital = expenses_payroll@token:market_capital }

			set_variable = { productivity@token:market_capital = controller:trade_productivity }
			
			set_variable = { base_productivity@token:market_capital = controller:trade_productivity }
			divide_variable = { base_productivity@token:market_capital = 7 } # 5*0.9 (workers) + 25*0.1 (elites)
		}
	}

	infrastructure_update = {
		set_variable = { roads_max_size = 10 } #Based on Tech

		set_variable = { highways_max_size = 10 } #Based on tech

		set_variable = { rail_max_size = 10 } #Based on tech

		set_variable = { waterways_max_size = navigable_rivers }
		add_to_variable = { waterways_max_size = unnavigable_rivers }

		if = {
			limit = {
				is_coastal = yes
			}
			set_variable = { port_max_size = 10 } #Based on tech
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = { port_size = 0 }
			set_variable = { port_max_size = 0 }
		}

		set_variable = { airport_max_size = 10 } #Based on tech

		set_temp_variable = { roads_building_slots_temp = roads_size }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { roads_building_slots_temp = roads_building_slots }
		add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = roads_building_slots_temp
		add_to_temp_variable = { roads_building_slots_temp = roads_building_slots }
		set_variable = { roads_building_slots = roads_building_slots_temp }

		set_temp_variable = { waterways_building_slots_temp = waterways_size }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { waterways_building_slots_temp = waterways_building_slots }
		add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = waterways_building_slots_temp
		add_to_temp_variable = { waterways_building_slots_temp = waterways_building_slots }
		set_variable = { waterways_building_slots = waterways_building_slots_temp }

	}
